2025-01-09T17:51:16Z #11 168.5 To enable it, please set the environment variable
2025-01-09T17:51:16Z #11 168.5 OMPI_MCA_opal_cuda_support=true
2025-01-09T17:51:16Z #11 168.5 before launching your MPI processes.
2025-01-09T17:51:16Z #11 168.5 Equivalently, you can set the MCA parameter in the command line:
2025-01-09T17:51:16Z #11 168.5 mpiexec --mca opal_cuda_support 1 ...
2025-01-09T17:51:16Z #11 168.5 Note that you might also need to set UCX_MEMTYPE_CACHE=n for CUDA awareness via
2025-01-09T17:51:16Z #11 168.5 UCX. Please consult UCX documentation for further details.
